City</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">NORWALK, Conn., March&#160;24, 2022 - FactSet (&#34;FactSet&#34; or the &#8220;Company&#8221;) (NYSE&#58;FDS) (NASDAQ&#58;FDS), a global provider of integrated financial information, analytical applications, and industry-leading service, today announced results for its second quarter ended February&#160;28, 2022. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;margin-top:15pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Second Quarter Fiscal 2022 Highlights</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Revenues</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> increased 10.0%, or $39.3 million, to $431.1 million for the second quarter of fiscal 2022 compared with $391.8 million for the same period in fiscal 2021. The increase was primarily due to higher sales of research and advisory and analytics solutions. Organic revenue, which excludes the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed within the last 12 months and foreign currency movements, grew 9.9% to $430.8 million during the second quarter of fiscal 2022 from the prior year period. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Annual Subscription Value</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> (ASV) plus professional services was $1.8 billion at February&#160;28, 2022, compared with $1.6 billion at February&#160;28, 2021. </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Organic ASV plus professional services, </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">which excludes the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed within the last 12 months and foreign currency movements,</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> was $1.7 billion at February&#160;28, 2022, up $146.3 million from the prior year at a growth rate of 9.4%. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Organic ASV </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">plus professional services increased $44.8 million over the last three months.</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> The primary contributors to this growth were higher sales of research and advisory and analytics solutions. Please see the &#8220;ASV + Professional Services&#8221; section of this press release for details.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Operating margin </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">decreased to 28.6% compared with 29.6% for the same period last year, driven by charges related to vacating certain leased office space and costs related to the CUSIP Global Services (CGS) acquisition, partially offset by growth in revenues, lower compensation costs and computer depreciation. Adjusted operating margin improved to 33.7% compared with 32.6% in the prior year period, primarily due to lower compensation expenses and decreased data costs</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Diluted earnings per share </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">(EPS) increased 13.6% to $2.84 compared with $2.50 for the same period in fiscal 2021. Adjusted diluted EPS increased 20.2% to $3.27 compared with the prior year period, primarily due to higher revenues, margin expansion and a decreased tax rate. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">EBITDA</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> increased to $146.8 million, up 11.1% for the second quarter of fiscal 2022, compared with $132.2 million for the same period in fiscal 2021. FactSet is providing this metric to allow additional transparency for its equity and debt investors.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">The Company&#8217;s</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:133%"> effective tax rate</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> for the second quarter decreased to 9.9% compared with 15.7% a year ago, primarily due to lower projected levels of income before income taxes and a tax provision reduction related to the lower rate compared with the three months ended February&#160;28, 2021. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">FactSet completed its acquisition of CGS, a standard in the global securities marketplace, on March 1, 2022. Related to the acquisition, on March 1, 2022, FactSet issued its inaugural investment grade senior notes consisting of $500 million principal amount of 2.90% senior notes due 2027 and $500 million principal amount of 3.45% senior notes due 2032. In addition, on March 1, 2022, FactSet entered into a new credit agreement providing for term and revolving credit facilities. </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:7pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">1</font></div><div style="padding-right:18pt"><font style="color:#dcdcdc;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:6pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:86.4pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">News Release </font><font style="color:#98ca3c;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">I</font><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> For Immediate Release</font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">FactSet updated its annual outlook for fiscal 2022. Please see the &#8220;Annual Business Outlook&#8221; section of this press release for details.</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:132%">&#8220;I&#8217;m pleased to report that FactSet once again delivered impressive quarterly results, reflecting the continuing momentum in our business,&#8221; said Phil Snow, CEO, FactSet. &#8220;The investments we have made are paying off in our top line growth. Demand for differentiated content remains strong, which we intend to build upon with our leading open content and analytics platform. In addition, we welcome the CGS business to FactSet, which will continue to advance our data management strategy.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Annual Subscription Value (ASV) + Professional Services </font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV at any given point in time represents the forward-looking revenues for the next twelve months from all subscription services currently supplied to clients. Professional services is revenue derived from project-based consulting and implementation.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV plus professional services was $1,750 million at February&#160;28, 2022 compared with $1,598 million at </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">February&#160;28, 2021</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">. Organic ASV plus professional services was $1,744 million at February&#160;28, 2022, up $146.3 million from the prior year at a growth rate of 9.4%. Organic ASV, which excludes the effects of acquisitions and dispositions </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">completed within the last 12 months</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> and foreign currency movements, plus professional services, increased $44.8 million over the last three months. </font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Buy-side and sell-side organic ASV growth rates for the second quarter of fiscal 2022 were 8.4% and 12.6%, respectively. Buy-side clients, who primarily include asset managers, asset owners, wealth managers, hedge funds, corporations, and channel partners, accounted for approximately 84% of organic ASV while the remainder came from sell-side firms that include broker-dealers, banking and advisory, private equity and venture capital firms. Supplementary tables covering organic buy-side and sell-side ASV growth rates may be found on the last page of this press release. </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:right"><font prior year period of </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">$985.2 million.</font><font Organic ASV increased 7.8% to $459.6 million. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">EMEA revenues were $114.6 million compared with $105.5 million in the second quarter of fiscal 2021. Organic ASV increased 14.3% to $180.9 million. Asia Pacific revenues were $42.9 million compared with $38.3 million in the second quarter of fiscal 2021. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Excluding the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed in the last 12 months and foreign currency impacts, the Asia Pacific region organic revenues growth rate was 13.7%. </font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Segment ASV does not include professional services, which totaled $24.2 million at February&#160;28, 2022.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;margin-top:15pt"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Operational Highlights &#8211; Second Quarter Fiscal 2022</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Client count as of February&#160;28, 2022 was 7,172, a net increase of 413 clients in the past three months, primarily driven by an increase in corporate clients. The count includes clients with ASV of $10,000 and more.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">User count increased by 9,180 to 171,341 in the past three months, primarily driven by an increase in research and advisory users.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Annual ASV retention was greater than 95%. FactSet anticipates additional impairment charges over the remainder of fiscal year 2022 in relation to exiting office space in several locations and expects these charges in the third fiscal quarter to total approximately $45 million. In addition, the Company incurred $5 million in expenses related to the CGS acquisition in the second quarter and anticipates an additional $14 million of acquisition expenses in the third quarter.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Employee count was 10,784 as of February&#160;28, 2022, up 1.2% over the last twelve months, primarily driven by increased hiring in the Company's content and technology organizations.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Net cash provided by operating activities decreased to $122.0 million compared with $140.7 million for the second quarter of fiscal 2021, primarily due to higher estimated tax payments. Quarterly free cash flow decreased to $110.1 million compared with $130.2 million a year ago, a decrease of 15.5%, primarily due to higher estimated tax payments.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">A quarterly dividend of $31.1 million, or $0.82 per share, was paid on March 17, 2022 to holders of record of FactSet&#8217;s common stock at the close of business on February&#160;28, 2022. </font></div><div style="padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">FactSet completed the acquisition of CGS for $1.925 billion in cash on March 1, 2022. The acquisition is expected to significantly expand FactSet&#8217;s critical role in the global capital markets. As part of FactSet, CGS will continue to carefully steward the CUSIP system in close partnership with the American Bankers Association. FactSet&#8217;s financial results will include CGS, which will function as a part of FactSet&#8217;s Content and Technology Solutions (CTS) business.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">FactSet closed its offering of $500 million principal amount of 2.90% senior notes due 2027 and $500 million principal amount of 3.45% senior notes due 2032 (both rated investment grade) and entered into new term and revolving credit facilities on March 1, 2022. Adjusted operating income and margin, adjusted net income, EBITDA, and adjusted diluted earnings per share exclude intangible asset amortization, the impact of the fair valuing of deferred revenues acquired in a business combination and non-recurring items. The Company believes that these adjusted financial measures better reflect the underlying economic performance of FactSet.</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Cash flows provided by operating activities, has been reduced by capital expenditures to report non-GAAP free cash flow.
